[*4816] Catzcute4: Brain tumors that start as a growth of cells in the brain are called primary brain tumors. They might start right in the brain or in the tissue nearby. Nearby tissue includes the membranes that cover the brain, called meninges. Brain tumors also can happen in nerves, the pituitary gland and the pineal gland.  Brain tumors happen when there are changes in the DNA of the cells in or near the brain.
